   <section class="content-area" id="ContentAreaHome">
    <div class="full">
     <div class="flex">
      <article class="content two-thirds" data-content="true">
       <div class="content-style" id="MainContent">
        <h1>
         <strong>
          <em>
           Welcome to
          </em>
          <br/>
          RWJBarnabas Health
         </strong>
        </h1>
        <p class="text-highlight t1">
         We provide our communities and patients convenient access to high-quality,
	 cost-efficient, coordinated healthcare.
        </p>
        <p>
         Our dedication to serving the people of New Jersey extends far beyond the
	 care we provide within our hospital walls. We support programs that promote
	 health and wellness in our communities and provide access to services
	 that would otherwise be unavailable. We are committed to the ongoing improvement
	 of the health, quality of life, and vitality of our communities. We strive
	 to bring the best healthcare to meet the evolving needs of residents in
	 New Jersey—whether that be enhancing the coordination for treating
	 complex health conditions or improving community health through local
	 programs and education.
        </p>
        <p>
         Once consummated, our planned partnership with Rutgers University will
	 create the state’s largest academic healthcare system dedicated
	 to providing high-quality patient care, leading-edge research, and world-class
	 health and medical education, further advancing our mission of providing
	 high-quality healthcare in New Jersey.
        </p>
        <p>
         The new collaboration also will align RWJBarnabas Health with Rutgers’
	 education, research, and clinical activities, including those at the
         <a href="http://www.cinj.org/" target="_blank">
          Rutgers Cancer Institute of New Jersey
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://ubhc.rutgers.edu/" target="_blank">
          Rutgers University Behavioral Health Care
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <!-- 
<p style="text-align:center;">
	<a href="/our-locations/"><img alt="undefined" src="/images/press/RWJBHInfo-org-600x350-new.jpg"></a>
</p>-->
        <h2 class="large" style="text-align:center;">
         Let's Be Healthy Together
        </h2>
        <style type="text/css">
         .content-area .announce-container{margin-bottom:9em;}
        </style>
       </div>
       <div aria-pressed="false" class="read-more" role="button" tabindex="0">
        <a class="show-more" href="javascript:void(0)">

          Read More
         </span>

          Show Less
         </span>

           <use xlink:href="/cms/svg/4joobvvc5i2.svg#icon_57598">
           </use>
          </svg>
         </icon>
        </a>
